   <script>
    /*! loadCSS. [c]2017 Filament Group, Inc. MIT License */
             (function(w){
                 "use strict";
                 /* exported loadCSS */
                 var loadCSS = function( href, before, media ){
                     // Arguments explained:
                     // `href` [REQUIRED] is the URL for your CSS file.
                     // `before` [OPTIONAL] is the element the script should use as a reference for injecting our stylesheet <link> before
                     // By default, loadCSS attempts to inject the link after the last stylesheet or script in the DOM. However, you might desire a more specific location in your document.
                     // `media` [OPTIONAL] is the media type or query of the stylesheet. By default it will be 'all'
                     var doc = w.document;
                     var ss = doc.createElement( "link" );
                     var ref;
                     if( before ){
                         ref = before;
                     }
                     else {
                         var refs = ( doc.body || doc.getElementsByTagName( "head" )[ 0 ] ).childNodes;
                         ref = refs[ refs.length - 1];
                     }
 
                     var sheets = doc.styleSheets;
                     ss.rel = "stylesheet";
                     ss.href = href;
                     // temporarily set media to something inapplicable to ensure it'll fetch without blocking render
                     ss.media = "only x";
 
                     // wait until body is defined before injecting link. This ensures a non-blocking load in IE11.
                     function ready( cb ){
                         if( doc.body ){
                             return cb();
                         }
                         setTimeout(function(){
                             ready( cb );
                         });
                     }
                     // Inject link
                     // Note: the ternary preserves the existing behavior of "before" argument, but we could choose to change the argument to "after" in a later release and standardize on ref.nextSibling for all refs
                     // Note: `insertBefore` is used instead of `appendChild`, for safety re: http://www.paulirish.com/2011/surefire-dom-element-insertion/
                     ready( function(){
                         ref.parentNode.insertBefore( ss, ( before ? ref : ref.nextSibling ) );
                     });
                     // A method (exposed on return object for external use) that mimics onload by polling document.styleSheets until it includes the new sheet.
                     var onloadcssdefined = function( cb ){
                         var resolvedHref = ss.href;
                         var i = sheets.length;
                         while( i-- ){
                             if( sheets[ i ].href === resolvedHref ){
                                 return cb();
                             }
                         }
                         setTimeout(function() {
                             onloadcssdefined( cb );
                         });
                     };
 
                     function loadCB(){
                         if( ss.addEventListener ){
                             ss.removeEventListener( "load", loadCB );
                         }
                         ss.media = media || "all";
                     }
 
                     // once loaded, set link's media back to `all` so that the stylesheet applies once it loads
                     if( ss.addEventListener ){
                         ss.addEventListener( "load", loadCB);
                     }
                     ss.onloadcssdefined = onloadcssdefined;
                     onloadcssdefined( loadCB );
                     return ss;
                 };
                 // commonjs
                 if( typeof exports !== "undefined" ){
                     exports.loadCSS = loadCSS;
                 }
                 else {
                     w.loadCSS = loadCSS;
                 }
             }( typeof global !== "undefined" ? global : this ));
 
             /*! loadCSS rel=preload polyfill. [c]2017 Filament Group, Inc. MIT License */
             (function( w ){
                 // rel=preload support test
                 if( !w.loadCSS ){
                     return;
                 }
                 var rp = loadCSS.relpreload = {};
                 rp.support = function(){
                     try {
                         return w.document.createElement( "link" ).relList.supports( "preload" );
                     } catch (e) {
                         return false;
                     }
                 };
 
                 // loop preload links and fetch using loadCSS
                 rp.poly = function(){
                     var links = w.document.getElementsByTagName( "link" );
                     for( var i = 0; i < links.length; i++ ){
                         var link = links[ i ];
                         if( link.rel === "preload" && link.getAttribute( "as" ) === "style" ){
                             w.loadCSS( link.href, link, link.getAttribute( "media" ) );
                             link.rel = null;
                         }
                     }
                 };
 
                 // if link[rel=preload] is not supported, we must fetch the CSS manually using loadCSS
                 if( !rp.support() ){
                     rp.poly();
                     var run = w.setInterval( rp.poly, 300 );
                     if( w.addEventListener ){
                         w.addEventListener( "load", function(){
                             rp.poly();
                             w.clearInterval( run );
                         } );
                     }
                     if( w.attachEvent ){
                         w.attachEvent( "onload", function(){
                             w.clearInterval( run );
                         } );
                     }
                 }
             }( this ));
   </script>

      <div class="promotion-content">
       <div class="content">
        <h3>
         session - Webshop für Musikinstrumente und Equipment
        </h3>
        <p>
         Auf session.de findest du unseren Webshop für Musikinstrumente, Equipment und Zubehör aus den Bereichen
         <a href="https://www.session.de/Tasteninstrumente/" title="">
          Tasteninstrumente
         </a>
         ,

         </a>

         <a href="https://www.session.de/Baesse/" title="">

         </a>
         ,

         </a>
         ,
         <a href="https://www.session.de/PA/" title="">

         </a>

         </a>
         ,
         <a href="https://www.session.de/Recording/" title="">
          Recording
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="https://www.session.de/Computer/" title="">
          Computer
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="https://www.session.de/DJ/" title="">
          DJ
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="https://www.session.de/Licht/" title="">
          Licht
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="https://www.session.de/Zubehoer/" title="">

         </a>
         sowie
         <a href="https://www.session.de/Noten-musikinstrumente/" title="">
          Noten, Bücher und Medien
         </a>
         .
         Im
         <a href="https://www.session.de/music/blog/?utm_campaign=startseite&amp;utm_source=box14_1&amp;utm_medium=1" target="_blank">
          session Blog
         </a>
         gibt es Artikel und Videos rund um Musik und Musik machen. Ab sofort gibt es auch die session-App
         für
         <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/de/app/session/id636818752?mt=8?utm_campaign=startseite&amp;utm_source=box14_2&amp;utm_medium=1" target="_blank">
          iPhone und iPad in Apples App-Store
         </a>
         sowie
         <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.sessionmusic&amp;feature=search_result#?t=W251bGwsMSwyLDEsImNvbS5zZXNzaW9ubXVzaWMiXQ&amp;utm_campaign=startseite&amp;utm_source=box14_3&amp;utm_medium=1" target="_blank">
          für Android-Geräte im Google Play Store
         </a>
         . Mit ihr kannst du auch unterwegs bequem in unserem Webshop stöbern und Musikinstrumente und Equipment einkaufen.

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var Mojo = {},
         captchasToRender = [];
 
     function captchaCallback()
     {
         for(var i = 0; i < captchasToRender.length; i++)
         {
             captchasToRender[i]();
         }
     };
 
     Mojo.popupManager = {};
 
     Mojo.addCaptchaToRender = function(id, siteKey, formSelector, popupId) {
 
         var recaptchaIsFinished = false;
 
         $(formSelector).submit(function(e)
         {
             if(!recaptchaIsFinished)
             {
                 $('#'+id+'-error').css('display', 'block');
                 e.preventDefault();
                 return false;
             }
         });
 
         $(formSelector).find(':submit').prop('disabled', false);
 
         if(popupId)
         {
             if(!Mojo.popupManager[popupId])
             {
                 Mojo.popupManager[popupId] = {hasLoaded: false, callbacks: [], recaptchaIsFinished: false};
                 $('#'+popupId).one('shown.bs.modal', function (e) {
                     if(!Mojo.popupManager[popupId].hasLoaded)
                     {
                         Mojo.popupManager[popupId].hasLoaded = true;
                         for(var i = 0; i < Mojo.popupManager[popupId].callbacks.length; i++)
                         {
                             Mojo.popupManager[popupId].callbacks[i]();
                         }
                     }
                 });
             }
             Mojo.popupManager[popupId].callbacks.push(function(){grecaptcha.render(id, {'sitekey': siteKey, 'callback': function(){ recaptchaIsFinished = true; $('#'+id+'-error').css('display', 'none'); $(formSelector).find(':submit').prop('disabled', false);} });  });
 
         }
         else
         {
             captchasToRender.push(function() {
                 grecaptcha.render(id, {'sitekey': siteKey, 'callback': function(){ recaptchaIsFinished = true; $('#'+id+'-error').css('display', 'none'); $(formSelector).find(':submit').prop('disabled', false);} });
             });
         }
     };
 
     window.onload = captchaCallback;
 
     function addRecaptchaScript() {
         var s = document.createElement('script');
         s.type = 'text/javascript';
         s.async = true;
         s.src = 'https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js?hl=de';
         var x = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
         x.parentNode.insertBefore(s, x);
     };
   </script>

                 'eventCategory': 'Navigation',
                 'eventAction': 'Klick',
                 'eventLabel': label,
             });
         }
     });
 
     
     
     
     
 
 
 });

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $.fn.isOnScreen = function(){
   if (this.length > 0) {
     var win = $(window);
 
     var viewport = {
         top : win.scrollTop(),
         left : win.scrollLeft()
     };
     viewport.right = viewport.left + win.width();
     viewport.bottom = viewport.top + win.height();
 
     var bounds = this.offset();
     bounds.right = bounds.left + this.outerWidth();
     bounds.bottom = bounds.top + this.outerHeight();
 
     return (!(viewport.right < bounds.left || viewport.left > bounds.right || viewport.bottom < bounds.top || viewport.top > bounds.bottom));
   }
 };
 
 String.prototype.filename=function(extension){
     var s= this.replace(/\\/g, '/');
     s= s.substring(s.lastIndexOf('/')+ 1);
     return extension? s.replace(/[?#].+$/, ''): s.split('.')[0];
 }
 
 $( document ).ready(function() {
 
   //Tracking vars
   var gtmPromotions = [];
   var gtmProducts = [];
   var trackElement;
   var src;
   var trackId;
   var dataToPush = 0;
 
   //Shown Banner
   var secondaryBannerShown = 0;
   var promotionBannerShown = 0;
   var categoryBannerShown = 0;
   var searchCategoryBannerShown = 0;
 
 if ($('#banner-slider').isOnScreen() && $('#banner-slider').find('.slick-track').find('.slick-active').find('img').attr('data-gtm-tracking-shown') != 'true') {
   trackElement = $('#banner-slider').find('.slick-track').find('.slick-active').find('img');
   src = trackElement.attr('src');
   trackId = trackElement.attr('alt');
 
   gtmPromotions.push({
                        id: trackId,
                        name: src.filename(),
                        creative: 'sliderTeaser',
                        position: 'slot'+trackElement.parent().attr('data-slick-index')
                      });
 
   $('#banner-slider').find('.slick-track').find('.slick-active').find('img').attr('data-gtm-tracking-shown', 'true');
   dataToPush = 1;
 }
 
 if ($('.secondary-banner').isOnScreen() && secondaryBannerShown === 0) {
   trackElement = $('.secondary-banner').find('img');
   src = trackElement.attr('src');
   trackId = trackElement.attr('alt');
 
   gtmPromotions.push({
                        id: trackId,
                        name: src.filename(),
                        creative: 'staticTeaser',
                        position: 'slot1'
                      });
 
   secondaryBannerShown = 1;
   dataToPush = 1;
 }
 
 if ($('.promotion-banners').isOnScreen() && promotionBannerShown === 0) {
   trackElement = $('.promotion-banners').find('img');
 
   $.each(trackElement, function(key, value) {
     src = trackElement[key].src;
     trackId = trackElement[key].alt;
 
     gtmPromotions.push({
                          id: trackId,
                          name: src.filename(),
                          creative: 'staticTeaser',
                          position: 'slot1'
                        });
   });
 
   promotionBannerShown = 1;
   dataToPush = 1;
 }
 
 if ($('.category-info').find('img').isOnScreen() && categoryBannerShown === 0){
   trackElement = $('.category-info').find('img');
   src = trackElement.attr('src');
   trackId = trackElement.attr('alt');
 
   gtmPromotions.push({
                        id: trackId,
                        name: src.filename(),
                        creative: 'staticTeaser',
                        position: 'slot1'
                      });
 
   categoryBannerShown = 1;
   dataToPush = 1;
 }
 
 if ($('.category-banner').isOnScreen() && searchCategoryBannerShown === 0){
   trackElement = $('.category-banner').find('img');
   src = trackElement.attr('src');
   trackId = trackElement.attr('alt');
 
   gtmPromotions.push({
                        id: trackId,
                        name: src.filename(),
                        creative: 'staticTeaser',
                        position: 'slot1'
                      });
 
   searchCategoryBannerShown = 1;
   dataToPush = 1;
 }
 
 if (dataToPush === 1) {
   dataLayer.push({
       'event': 'EECpromotionImpression',
       'ecommerce': {
           'promoView': {
               'promotions': gtmPromotions
           }

   });
   dataToPush = 0;
   gtmPromotions = [];
 }
 
 $(window).scroll(function () {
     if (scrollTimeout) {
         clearTimeout(scrollTimeout);
         scrollTimeout = null;
     }
     var scrollTimeout = setTimeout(scrollHandlerPromotions, 250);
 });

 function formatPrice( price, vat ){
     var pre = price.split('€');
     var result = pre[1].trim().split(',-');
     
     if (vat == '7') {
         var formatedVat = 1.07;
     } else if (vat == '19') {
         var formatedVat = 1.19;
     } else {
         var formatedVat = 0;
     }
 
     if (result[0].indexOf('.') != -1) {
         var formatedResult = result[0].replace('.','');
     } else {
         var formatedResult = result[0];
     }
 
     var fprice = formatedResult.replace(',','.') / formatedVat;
     var rounded = Math.round(fprice * 100) / 100;
 
     return rounded.toString();
 }
 
 function formatListPosition( position ){
   var pre = position.split('_');
   return parseInt(pre[1])
 }
 
 function checkProductBadge( arrayElement, condition ){
   if (condition === 'hot'){
     if ($(arrayElement).find('.hot-article').length > 0) {
       return 'ja';
     } else {
       return 'nein';
     }
   } else if (condition === 'sale'){
     if ($(arrayElement).find('.sale-article').length > 0) {
       return 'ja';
     } else {
       return 'nein';
     }
   } else if (condition === 'new'){
     if ($(arrayElement).find('.new-article').length > 0) {
       return 'ja';
     } else {
       return 'nein';
     }
   }
 }
 
 function trackProductSlider( elementName ){
   trackElement = $(elementName).find('.slick-track').find('.slick-active');
   $.each(trackElement, function(key, value) {
     if ($(elementName).isOnScreen() && $(trackElement[key]).attr('data-gtm-tracking-shown') != 'true'){
       listname = $(elementName).find('h3').text();
 
         gtmProducts.push({
                             name: $(trackElement[key]).find('.product-overview').attr('data-gtm-productname'),
                             id: $(trackElement[key]).find('.product-overview').attr('data-gtm-productid'),
                             price: formatPrice($(trackElement[key].innerHTML).find('.price').text().trim(), $(trackElement[key]).find('.product-overview').attr('data-gtm-vat')),
                             brand: $(trackElement[key]).find('.product-overview').attr('data-gtm-manufacturer'),
                             list: listname,
                             position: parseInt($(trackElement[key]).attr('data-slick-index')),
                             dimension7: checkProductBadge(trackElement[key],'sale'),
                             dimension8: checkProductBadge(trackElement[key],'hot'),
                             dimension9: checkProductBadge(trackElement[key],'new'),
                            });
 
         $(trackElement[key]).attr('data-gtm-tracking-shown', 'true');
 
 
 
       dataToPush = 1;
     }
   });
 }
 
 function trackProductList( elementName ){
   trackElement = $(elementName).find('.product-list').children('li');
   $.each(trackElement, function(key, value) {
     if ($(trackElement[key]).isOnScreen() && $(trackElement[key]).attr('data-gtm-tracking-shown') != 'true'){
       listname = $('.category-content').text().trim();
 
         gtmProducts.push({
                             name: $(trackElement[key]).find('.product').attr('data-gtm-productname'),
                             id: $(trackElement[key]).find('.product').attr('data-article-id'),
                             price: formatPrice($(trackElement[key].innerHTML).find('.price').text().trim(), $(trackElement[key]).find('.product').attr('data-gtm-vat')),
                             brand: $(trackElement[key]).find('.product').attr('data-gtm-manufacturer'),
                             list: listname,
                             position: formatListPosition($(trackElement[key].innerHTML).find('.product-link').attr('id')),
                             dimension7: checkProductBadge(trackElement[key],'sale'),
                             dimension8: checkProductBadge(trackElement[key],'hot'),
                             dimension9: checkProductBadge(trackElement[key],'new'),
                            });
 
         $(trackElement[key]).attr('data-gtm-tracking-shown', 'true');
 
 
 
       dataToPush = 1;
     }
   });
 }
 
 function pushProductImpressions(){
   if (dataToPush === 1) {
     dataLayer.push({
         'event': 'EECproductImpression',
         'ecommerce': {
             'impressions': gtmProducts
         }
     });
     dataToPush = 0;
     gtmProducts = [];
   }
 }
 
 
 //HOT-article-slider
 trackProductSlider('.hot-articles');
 
 $('#hot-article-slider').on('init', onHotArticlesInitialized());
 
 function onHotArticlesInitialized(){
   $('#hot-article-slider .slick-next').click(function(e){
     trackProductSlider('.hot-articles');
     pushProductImpressions();
   });
   $('#hot-article-slider .slick-prev').click(function(e){
     trackProductSlider('.hot-articles');
     pushProductImpressions();
   });
 }

   $('#recommendations-slider .slick-next').click(function(e){
     trackProductSlider('.econda-recommendations');

         clearTimeout(scrollTimeout);
         scrollTimeout = null;
     }
     var scrollTimeout = setTimeout(scrollHandlerProducts, 250);
 });
 
 //Scroll-Tracking

   //HOT-article-slider
   trackProductSlider('.hot-articles');

     trackProductList('.products');
   }
 
   //Push dataLayer
   pushProductImpressions();
 };$('.product').click( function(e){
   if ($(this).hasClass('slick-slide') && $(this).hasClass('product')) {
     dataLayer.push({
       'event': 'EECproductClick',
       'ecommerce': {
           'click': {
               'actionField': {'list': $(this).parent().parent().parent().parent().parent().parent().find('h3').text()},
               'products': [{
                   'name': $(this).find('.product-overview').attr('data-gtm-productname'),
                   'id': $(this).find('.product-overview').attr('data-gtm-productid'),
                   'price': formatPrice($(this).find('.price').text().trim(), $(this).find('.product-overview').attr('data-gtm-vat')),
                   'brand': $(this).find('.product-overview').attr('data-gtm-manufacturer'),
                   'position': parseInt($(this).attr('data-slick-index')),
                   'dimension7': checkProductBadge($(this),'sale'),
                   'dimension8': checkProductBadge($(this),'hot'),
                   'dimension9': checkProductBadge($(this),'new')
               }]
           }
       }
     });
   } else {
     dataLayer.push({
       'event': 'EECproductClick',
       'ecommerce': {
           'click': {
               'actionField': {'list': $('.category-content').text().trim()},
               'products': [{
                   'name': $(this).attr('data-gtm-productname'),
                   'id': $(this).attr('data-article-id'),
                   'price': formatPrice($(this).find('.price').text().trim(), $(this).attr('data-gtm-vat')),
                   'brand': $(this).attr('data-gtm-manufacturer'),
                   'position': formatListPosition($(this).find('.product-link').attr('id')),
                   'dimension7': checkProductBadge($(this),'sale'),
                   'dimension8': checkProductBadge($(this),'hot'),
                   'dimension9': checkProductBadge($(this),'new')
               }]
           }
       }
     });
   }
 });
 });

 $(document).ready(function(){
         var categoryId = "",
         parent = "start",
         baseUrl = "https://www.session.de/",
         onMobileNavigationLoaded = function(mobileNavigation) {
             $('#mobile-navigation .mobile-category-navigation-tree').html(mobileNavigation);
             initMobileNavigation();
         };
 
         expandCurrentCategories = function() {
             var currentLink = $($('.category-list a[data-category-id="'+categoryId+'"]'));
             currentLink.addClass('active');
 
             var parentCategoryNodes = currentLink.parents('.category-list [data-category-id]');
             for(var i = 0; i < parentCategoryNodes.length;i++) {
                 var listElement = $(parentCategoryNodes[i]);
                 listElement.addClass('jstree-open');
                 $(listElement.find('> a')).addClass('active');
             }
         }
 
         initMobileNavigation = function() {
             expandCurrentCategories();
             $('#mobile-navigation .mobile-main-navigation-tree').jstree();
             $('#mobile-navigation .mobile-category-navigation-tree').jstree();
 
             var wantToOpenMenu = false;
             $('#open-mobile-menu, .show-all-categories-button').on('click', function () {
                 $('#curtain').addClass('active');
                 $('#mobile-navigation').addClass('active');
                 wantToOpenMenu = true;
             });
 
             $('#mobile-navigation').on('clickoutside', function (e) {
                 setTimeout(function () {
                     if (!wantToOpenMenu) {
                         $('#curtain').removeClass('active');
                         $('#mobile-navigation').removeClass('active');
                     }
                     wantToOpenMenu = false;
                 }, 10);
             });
 
 
             $('#mobile-navigation-close-button').on('click', function () {
                 $('#curtain').removeClass('active');
                 $('#mobile-navigation').removeClass('active');
             });
         };
 
 
 
                 initMobileNavigation();
         
 
     });

         clickedBasket = true;
